# PROJECT_STATE.md

`PROJECT_STATE.md` is the canonical truth source for checked-in facts. If chat history, summaries, or stale notes disagree with this file, this file wins.

## Locked Decisions
- `Meridian Alpha Platform` is the checked-in dual-track project name: `Agent Control Framework` plus `Research & Alpha Platform`.
- `EnhengClaw` remains a supported legacy compatibility identity for the existing Python package, external app directory, retained evidence paths, and `ENHENGCLAW_*` environment variables.
- The canonical new slug is `meridian_alpha`, and the canonical new environment prefix is `MERIDIAN_ALPHA_`.
- `Research & Alpha Platform` may depend on the governance/runtime framework; the framework track must not depend on quant research, scheduled tasks, or workbench-specific modules.
- `config/project_governance/project_profile.json` is the machine-readable project identity contract.
- `config/project_governance/stage_contract.json` is the machine-readable project stage contract.
- Current checked-in stage is `stage_4_automated_execution`.
- Target stage is `stage_4_automated_execution`.
- Real-24h permit margin is `86460.0` (`24h + 60s`).
- `real-24h acceptance`, `preflight-only`, the Python wrapper, the PowerShell entrypoint, `run_config`, and preflight evidence all use the same real-24h margin.
- `preflight-only` must write:
  - `run_config.json`
  - `preflight_result.json`
  - `provider_health_snapshot.json`
  - `preflight_assertions.json`
- `preflight_assertions.json.all_green = true` is the only rerun admission signal.
- Rerun is allowed only when:
  - `<ArtifactsRoot>\preflight_only\<PreflightLabel>\preflight_assertions.json` exists
  - `all_green = true`
  - `<RerunLabel> != <PreflightLabel>`
- Rerun verdict may read only the current `<ArtifactsRoot>\soak_runs\<RerunLabel>\` directory and only:
  - `go_no_go.json`
  - `soak_summary.json`
  - `provider_health_snapshot.json`
  - `audit_record.json`
- Real-24h rerun pass requires:
  - `READY_FOR_REAL_24H_SHADOW = true`
  - `READY_FOR_BROAD_AGENT_LAYER = true`
  - `agent_layer_governance.blockers = []`
  - `broad_blockers = []`
  - `current_controlled_slice_ids = ["market_observer", "attention_allocator", "evidence_agent", "research_lead", "research_synthesizer", "risk_governance_agent", "risk_signal_agent", "validation_agent"]`
  - `registered_pending_promotion_controlled_slice_ids = []`
  - `hard_failures = []`
  - `soft_failures = []`
  - `audit_record.status = "completed"`
  - `soak_summary.violations = []`
- Binance preflight structured diagnostics must include:
  - `failure_category`
  - `transport_stage`
  - `endpoint`
  - `transport`
  - `host`
  - `port`
  - `exception_type`
  - `exception_message`
  - `exception_chain`
- `READY_FOR_AGENT_LAYER` is computed from shadow-acceptance evidence plus `config/agent_layer_governance/manifest.json` and `config/agent_layer_governance/governed_slice_registry.json`.
- `READY_FOR_BROAD_AGENT_LAYER` is computed from shadow-acceptance evidence plus the checked-in broad-ready governance state.
- The checked-in owner topology contract uses one explicit owner: `rulebook_owner`.
- The machine-readable owner topology contract is `config/agent_architecture/main_owner_manifest.json`.
- The machine-readable runtime ownership contract is `config/project_governance/runtime_ownership_contract.json`.
- Current runtime ownership contract state is `runtime_ownership_phase = partial`, `owner_verification_required = true`, and `owner_verification_enforced_in_boundary_gates = true`.
- Six compatibility delegates still share `runtime.continue_existing_from_agent_payloads`; that is why the runtime ownership phase remains `partial` instead of claiming migration is complete.
- Boundary gates now execute owner-first verification checks before a governed write may claim `FINALIZED`, but that gate does not by itself retire the remaining compatibility delegates.
- Owner artifacts live under `RunArtifactsRoot\agent_owner\<run_id>\`; repo-local `artifacts\agent_owner\<run_id>\` is only one generated example.
- Quant promotion/export eligibility now comes from `RunArtifactsRoot\governance\promotion_decisions\<as_of>\<alpha_id>.promotion_decision.json`; alpha/status files remain descriptive and are not the export gate by themselves.
- Current quant bridge publication policy is governed by `config/quant_research/publication_contract.json`: Stage 0/1 are archive-only, deterministic outputs remain non-publishable, and live backend outputs may become publishable only after promotion-decision, hash/freshness, backend-mode, validation, and bridge-contract gates pass.
- The checked-in governed-slice registry currently admits `["market_observer", "evidence_agent", "risk_signal_agent", "risk_governance_agent", "validation_agent", "attention_allocator", "research_synthesizer", "research_lead"]`.
- The checked-in governance manifest currently allows all eight admitted slices and keeps the broad agent layer disabled by default even when broad-ready is `true`.
- OpenClaw external deployment remains intentionally narrow: `market_observer` is the only create-new lane, the other seven lanes are resume-only, and broad external rollout is still disabled.

## Required Preflight Assertions
- `execution_permit_path_exists`
- `explicit_execution_permit_supplied`
- `execution_permit_path_outside_repo`
- `execution_permit_path_not_temp`
- `permit_minimum_margin_seconds_ok`
- `trust_root_ok`
- `binance_preflight_passed`
- `alchemy_preflight_passed`
- `run_config_min_permit_margin_seconds_ok`
- `preflight_minimum_required_seconds_ok`
- `key_evidence_files_exist`
- `preflight_status_passed`

## Current Blockers
- Current stage profile is `stage_4_automated_execution`, which satisfies the stage-contract minimum for automated-execution review. This does not enable broad consumption or live order flow by itself: `broad_agent_layer_enabled=false`, owner/on-host gates, budget epochs, live-order gates, and fail-closed runtime controls still bind.
- Checked-in broad rollout remains disabled until a separate manifest unlock change explicitly flips it, and `config/agent_layer_governance/broad_unlock_contract.json` evaluates as eligible for manual unlock.
- Formal external OpenClaw deployment claims must not exceed the latest successful retained bundle from `python scripts\verify\run_openclaw_deployment_readiness.py --execution-permit <WindowsPermitPath> [...]`.
- Default OpenClaw operator workflow still depends on a valid external execution permit and the read-only `C:\ProgramData\EnhengClaw\trust` boundary.
- Provider and network availability must still hold on the target host for live bundles to succeed.
- Formal real-24h shadow claims must not exceed the latest successful full-duration retained bundle from `python scripts\verify\run_real_24h_shadow_bundle.py --execution-permit <WindowsPermitPath> --artifacts-root <ArtifactsRoot> --preflight-label <PreflightLabel> --rerun-label <RerunLabel> [--trust-root-dir <WindowsTrustRootDir>]`.
- The current repo-local and external research workflows do not unblock real-24h or broad rollout by themselves.
- Accepted evidence is freshness-gated. If a referenced bundle is older than `config/agent_layer_governance/evidence_freshness_contract.json`, lacks evidence metadata, or comes from a different source commit, it is historical evidence only and not a current readiness claim.
- The supported operator-host contract is still one Windows workstation plus WSL; Linux/macOS CI does not imply cross-platform operator deployment support.

## DTH60 -> 12-Factor P10 Live Integration (live stage advanced beyond P9DH)

- STATE-SYNC NOTE (2026-06-09): the DTH60/CoinGlass P9 ladder above (through P9DH) was the 5-factor-baseline candidate path. Live integration has since advanced to a distinct **P10 12-factor candidate** ladder that was committed but not previously recorded here, leaving this file stale at P9DH. This subsection records the P10 state derived from the committed P10 scripts (`scripts/live_trading/run_hv_balanced_12factor_p10*.py`, committed in `5f09cbc`, whose message "Add klines start and end time support" understates its scope) plus operator-reported live activity. Caveat: only `p10a`/`p10c` proof artifacts are retained in-repo under `artifacts/live_trading/hv_balanced_12factor_candidate/`; most P10 gate artifacts are generated per-run and are not committed, so the per-gate sha256 bundles that the P9 entries carry are not available here.
- Live alpha architecture: the live `frozen_config_path` baseline remains the 5-factor OHLCV `v5_binance_pit_top_mid_h10d_pruned3_hv_balanced_soft_budget`. The **12-factor candidate** `xs_alpha_ontology_v5_rw_bridge_no_overlay_lsk3_g_v2_h10d` (manifest `src/enhengclaw/quant_research/cross_sectional_hypothesis_batch_manifest_alpha_ontology_v5_rw_bridge_no_overlay_lsk3_g_v2_h10d.json`; alpha card `artifacts/quant_research/experiments/2026-04-29-xs_alpha_ontology_v5_rw_bridg-6054571c70ef/`) enters live execution as a **candidate-target-plan replacement** on that baseline, with hash binding, baseline fallback, and kill switch (P10G), using real CoinGlass derivatives features (funding/OI/taker/price) via a PIT-safe live feature builder (P10A). So "live config = 5-factor baseline" and "live-scored alpha = 12-factor candidate" are simultaneously true; 5-factor factor/risk audits elsewhere describe the baseline, not the live-scored candidate.
- P10 ladder (committed scripts): P10A PIT-safe live feature builder (real CoinGlass) -> P10C live-snapshot/research-input parity -> P10D default-off 12-factor scorer wrapper -> P10E live scorer entry -> P10F timer-path no-order shadow cycles -> P10G no-order candidate target-plan replacement dry-run -> P10H single-cycle live_delta canary terms owner gate -> P10I execute single-cycle live_delta canary (first 12-factor live order) -> P10J review -> P10K/P10L limited live_delta candidate executor-path discussion -> P10M-P10AK bundled corridors (followup proposal / execution terms / execution readiness / followup canary / limited live_delta expansion / limited execution terms / limited canary) -> P10AKR review of P10AK blocker resolution -> P10AKS-P10AKU revised nonflat terms corridor -> P10AKV-P10AKX read-only position-relation corridor -> P10AKY-P10ALA position-relation resolution corridor (latest). Current allowed next gate is `P10ALB_owner_select_candidate_position_relation_resolution_path_only_if_separately_requested`: the 12-factor candidate target sides conflict with the existing non-flat live book, and the owner must select one resolution path. These remain owner-gated, proof/local-first; order authority and continuous automated order flow are not authorized.
- Operator-reported live activity (not a retained P10 gate bundle; account-side evidence only): a NEAR/TRX leverage fix (20x->2x) was run prepare-only with `submitted_order_count=0`/`fill_count=0` (evidence `account_setting_preparation.json`); then a scaled entry/resize live delta (`sizing_multiplier=1.992`, projected `post_plan_available_balance_ratio=0.0506860869` just above the 5% floor) executed 10 fills with reconciliation complete, leaving `open_order_count=0`, `open_position_count=11`, `canTrade=true`, account after `available_balance_usdt=532.6243826`/`total_wallet_balance_usdt=10739.7403637` (evidence `entry_resize_scaled_live_execution_review_summary.json`). The strict post-run readback was blocked only by `timer_state_changed` (benign systemd timer ActiveState/SubState churn); the account side proved clean (canTrade=true, no open orders, zero new order/cancel/fill/trade delta) and the health monitor passed. This does not by itself approve Stage-4 automation, continuous order flow, timer-path load, or relax any fail-closed gate.
- Strategy-agnostic order-flow bounding for any future bounded-unattended run (aggregate budget, per-order notional ceiling, terminal disarm) was added DEFAULT-OFF this session (`unattended_budget_gate.py` / `unattended_budget_store.py` / `unattended_budget_hook.py`, `live_risk_controls.evaluate_per_order_notional_gate`, health-monitor terminal disarm); it composes under the candidate-replacement layer and is not enabled.
